<script>
webVitals.onINP(metric => {
    // Verificar se o valor do INP é superior a 200ms
    if (metric.value > 200) {
        console.log(`INP Valor: ${metric.value}ms`);

        // Verificar se há entradas (eventos) associados ao INP
        if (metric.entries && metric.entries.length > 0) {
            const entry = metric.entries[0]; // Considerando apenas a primeira entrada
            // Verificar se a entrada possui um alvo (elemento)
            if (entry.target) {
                // Obter apenas o HTML do elemento causador
                const targetHTML = entry.target.outerHTML;
                
                // Exibir o HTML do elemento causador
                console.log('HTML do Elemento Causador:', targetHTML);
            }
        }
    }
}, { reportAllChanges: true });
</script>

			$(window).load(function(){
			var leaderHeight = $("#zox-lead-top").outerHeight();
			var botHeight = $("#zox-bot-head-wrap").outerHeight();
			var navHeight = $("#zox-main-head-wrap").outerHeight();
			var headerHeight = navHeight + leaderHeight;
			var stickHeight = headerHeight - botHeight;

				var scroll = $(this).scrollTop();
				if ($(window).scrollTop() > headerHeight){
					$("#zox-bot-head-wrap").addClass("zox-fix-up");
					$("#zox-site-grid").css("margin-top", botHeight);
					$(".zox-post-soc-scroll").addClass("zox-post-soc-scroll-out");

					$("#zox-site-grid").css("margin-top", "0" );
